TITLE      Measurement of the prompt fission neutron spectrum     14829001    3 
           from 800 keV to 10 MeV for 240Pu(sf) and for the       14829001    4 
           240Pu(n,F) reaction induced by neutrons of energy      14829001    5 
           from 1-20 MeV                                          14829001    6 
AUTHOR     (K.J.Kelly,M.Devlin,J.M.O'Donnell,D.Neudecker,C.Y.Wu,  14829001    7 
           R.Henderson,A.E.Lovell,R.C.Haight,E.A.Bennett,         14829001    8 
           J.L.Ullmann,N.Fotiades,P.A.Copp)                       14829001    9 
REFERENCE  (J,PR/C,109,064611,2024)                               14829001   10 
           #doi:10.1103/PhysRevC.109.064611                       14829001   11 
REL-REF    (I,14682001,K.J.Kelly+,J,PR/C,102,034615,2020)         14829001   12 
INSTITUTE  (1USALAS,1USALRL)                                      14829001   13 
FACILITY   (LINAC,1USALAS) The high-energy Los Alamos Neutron     14829001   14 
           Science Center white neutron source at the Weapons     14829001   15 
           Neutron Research facility.                             14829001   16 
DETECTOR   (SCIN,PPAC) Neutrons were detected with a 54-element   14829001   17 
           EJ-309 liquid scintillator detector array Chi-Nu.      14829001   18 
SAMPLE     (94-PU-240,ENR=0.99875)                                14829001   19 
           (94-PU-242,ENR=0.00114) A parallel plate avalanche     14829001   20 
           counter (PPAC) target, fabricated at Lawrence          14829001   21 
           Livermore National Laboratory, containing              14829001   22 
           approximately 20 mg total of 99.875% pure 240Pu        14829001   23 
           located within the experimental flight path (WNR       14829001   24 
           FP15L). The remaining contributions to the total       14829001   25 
           target mass are 0.114% 242Pu, with all other isotopes  14829001   26 
           below 0.01%.                                           14829001   27 
METHOD     (TOF,PSD) Incident neutrons from 1.0-20.0 MeV were     14829001   28 
           measured via time of flight between a signal           14829001   29 
           corresponding to the spallation reaction time,         14829001   30 
           denoted t0, and a fission detection in the PPAC at a   14829001   31 
           time tf. The incident neutron flight path was          14829001   32 
           21.5(1) m, yielding flight times from 1483.94-281.39   14829001   33 
           ns for Einc n = 1.0-20.0 MeV.                          14829001   34 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Error propagation was used to calculate total  14829001   35 
           uncertainties from statistical and systematic.         14829001   36 
CORRECTION Corrections were applied to both the (n,f) and (sf)    14829001   37 
           liquid scintillator and PPAC data to eliminate signal  14829001   38 
           reflections within the cables, signal time walk, timing14829001   39 
            alignments of all detectors together, and to isolate  14829001   40 
           neutron signals from gamma rays using pulse-shape      14829001   41 
           discrimination (PSD), and further purify the neutron   14829001   42 
           signals using neutron kinematics relative to the       14829001   43 
           fission detection times.                               14829001   44
